<file path="cios-backend/prisma/schema.prisma">
// ============================================================================
// CIOS — Client Intelligence Operating System
// Prisma 7 Schema  |  PostgreSQL  |  pgvector + pg_search (ParadeDB)
// Schema v4.1 — 28 tables + refresh_tokens
//
// CHANGELOG v4.0 → v4.1
// ─────────────────────
// [CHANGE 1] UserRole enum: removed `project_owner`.
//            Project ownership is a relationship (projects.owner_id), not a
//            workspace-level role. A user can own Project A while being a
//            plain editor on Project B — a single UserRole value can't
//            express that. See User + Project models below.
//
// [CHANGE 2] RefreshToken table: KEPT (did not move to a 1:1 field on User).
//            Rationale documented on the model itself. TL;DR — a single
//            refresh_token column forces one active session per user, which
//            kills multi-device login, per-device revocation, and "log out
//            everywhere". The table has almost no operational overhead.
//
// [CHANGE 3] Project.fathom_link: String? → String[].
//            Fathom regenerates share URLs periodically, so a project
//            accumulates multiple links over time. Modeled as a text array.
//
// [CHANGE 4] ProjectMember: clarified the 1-to-many relationship intent in
//            comments. No structural change — the existing shape already
//            supports many memberships per user and enforces same-workspace
//            via workspace_id.
//
// [CHANGE 5] ProjectMember.access_level: String → new enum AccessLevel.
//            Values: read_only | edit. Replaces the free-text field.
//
// [CHANGE 6] ProjectDocument.{openai_file_id, anthropic_file_id,
//            vector_store_file_id}: kept, with expanded comments explaining
//            which provider path populates each and why all three are
//            justified by the BYOK + dual-provider ingestion plan.
//
// IMPORTANT — Three column types require raw SQL migrations (Prisma cannot
// generate DDL for these natively):
//   • pgvector `embedding vector(1536)` columns
//   • tsvector `content_search_vector` generated column on messages
//   • HNSW + BM25 indexes (Section 10 of schema doc)
// See the raw SQL reference block at the bottom of this file.
// ============================================================================

generator client {
  provider     = "prisma-client"
  output       = "../src/generated/prisma"
  moduleFormat = "cjs"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ENUMS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// [CHANGE 1] Removed `project_owner` from UserRole.
// Ownership of a specific project is tracked by projects.owner_id (FK → users.id).
// A user's workspace-level permission tier is orthogonal to which projects
// they happen to own.
enum UserRole {
  admin
  team_member
}

// [CHANGE 5] New enum for ProjectMember.access_level.
// Extend here if new tiers are needed (e.g. `comment_only`, `admin`).
enum AccessLevel {
  read_only
  edit
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.1  WORKSPACES — multi-tenant root entity
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Workspace {
  id         String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  name       String
  /// Workspace-level preferences (default model, branding, feature flags, etc.).
  /// Shape is intentionally loose so product can iterate without migrations.
  settings   Json?
  created_at DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at DateTime @updatedAt

  // ── reverse relations ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  users                     User[]
  projects                  Project[]
  project_members           ProjectMember[]
  project_custom_properties ProjectCustomProperty[]
  thread_groups             ThreadGroup[]
  threads                   Thread[]
  messages                  Message[]
  project_documents         ProjectDocument[]
  document_chunks           DocumentChunk[]
  attachments               Attachment[]
  vault_items               VaultItem[]
  skills                    Skill[]
  skill_versions            SkillVersion[]
  thread_active_skills      ThreadActiveSkill[]
  mcp_servers               McpServer[]
  artifact_templates        ArtifactTemplate[]
  document_templates        DocumentTemplate[]
  artifacts                 Artifact[]
  artifact_files            ArtifactFile[]
  scraping_events           ScrapingEvent[]
  usage_events              UsageEvent[]
  audit_log                 AuditLog[]
  api_keys                  ApiKey[]
  mentions                  Mention[]
  notifications             Notification[]
  // [WORKSPACE INVITE] Reverse relation — allows querying all invitations
  // sent from this workspace (e.g. to show pending invites in the admin panel).
  workspace_invitations     WorkspaceInvitation[]

  @@map("workspaces")
}

// ── [WORKSPACE INVITE] NEW ENUM ──────────────────────────────────────────────
// Lifecycle states for a workspace invitation record.
// pending  = email sent, user has not yet accepted
// accepted = user clicked the magic link and joined the workspace
enum InvitationStatus {
  pending
  accepted
}
// ── [WORKSPACE INVITE] END NEW ENUM ──────────────────────────────────────────

// ── [WORKSPACE INVITE] NEW MODEL ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tracks email invitations sent by admins to add new or existing users to a
// workspace. Each record stores the target email, the one-time token embedded
// in the magic link, and the current status (pending → accepted).
// No expiry — tokens remain valid until used.
model WorkspaceInvitation {
  id           String           @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String           @db.Uuid
  invited_by   String           @db.Uuid
  email        String
  token        String           @unique
  status       InvitationStatus @default(pending)
  created_at   DateTime         @default(now())
  updated_at   DateTime         @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  inviter   User      @relation("WorkspaceInvitationInvitedBy", fields: [invited_by], references: [id])

  @@index([workspace_id])
  @@index([token])
  @@map("workspace_invitations")
}
// ── [WORKSPACE INVITE] END NEW MODEL ─────────────────────────────────────────

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.2  USERS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model User {
  id               String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id     String?  @db.Uuid
  email            String   @unique
  password_hash    String?
  google_id        String?  @unique
  full_name        String?
  avatar_url       String?
  role             UserRole @default(team_member)
  is_active        Boolean  @default(true)
  default_model    String?
  /// Per-user UI state: sidebar layout, pinned projects, collapsed groups, etc.
  view_preferences Json?    @default("{}")
  created_at       DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at       DateTime @updatedAt

  workspace      Workspace?     @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  // [CHANGE 2] RefreshToken relation stays as 1-to-many (NOT 1-to-1).
  // One user may have many live refresh tokens — one per device/session.
  refresh_tokens RefreshToken[]
  // [WORKSPACE INVITE] Reverse relation — tracks all invitations this admin
  // user has sent. Named relation required because User has multiple FK
  // relationships to WorkspaceInvitation.
  sent_invitations WorkspaceInvitation[] @relation("WorkspaceInvitationInvitedBy")

  // Project ownership — named relation because User → Project has multiple FKs.
  owned_projects                Project[]          @relation("ProjectOwner")
  // Project memberships (member / assigned_by are different FKs → named relations)
  project_memberships           ProjectMember[]    @relation("MemberUser")
  assigned_memberships          ProjectMember[]    @relation("AssignedByUser")
  // Thread groups
  thread_groups_created         ThreadGroup[]      @relation("ThreadGroupCreatedBy")
  // Threads
  threads_created               Thread[]           @relation("ThreadCreatedBy")
  // Messages
  messages_created              Message[]          @relation("MessageCreatedBy")
  // Custom properties
  custom_properties_created     ProjectCustomProperty[] @relation("CustomPropertyCreatedBy")
  // Documents
  documents_uploaded            ProjectDocument[]  @relation("DocumentUploadedBy")
  // Vault items
  vault_items_uploaded          VaultItem[]        @relation("VaultItemUploadedBy")
  // Skills
  skills_created                Skill[]            @relation("SkillCreatedBy")
  skills_approved               Skill[]            @relation("SkillApprovedBy")
  skill_versions_changed        SkillVersion[]     @relation("SkillVersionChangedBy")
  // MCP servers
  mcp_servers_added             McpServer[]        @relation("McpAddedBy")
  mcp_servers_approved          McpServer[]        @relation("McpApprovedBy")
  // Artifact templates
  artifact_templates_created    ArtifactTemplate[] @relation("ArtifactTemplateCreatedBy")
  artifact_templates_approved   ArtifactTemplate[] @relation("ArtifactTemplateApprovedBy")
  // Document templates
  document_templates_created    DocumentTemplate[] @relation("DocumentTemplateCreatedBy")
  document_templates_approved   DocumentTemplate[] @relation("DocumentTemplateApprovedBy")
  // Attachments
  attachments_uploaded          Attachment[]       @relation("AttachmentUploadedBy")
  // Scraping / usage events
  scraping_events               ScrapingEvent[]    @relation("ScrapingEventUser")
  usage_events                  UsageEvent[]       @relation("UsageEventUser")
  // Audit log
  audit_log_entries             AuditLog[]         @relation("AuditLogUser")
  // API keys
  api_keys_added                ApiKey[]           @relation("ApiKeyAddedBy")
  // Mentions (mentioned vs mentioned_by → two named relations)
  received_mentions             Mention[]          @relation("MentionedUser")
  sent_mentions                 Mention[]          @relation("MentionedByUser")
  // Notifications
  notifications                 Notification[]     @relation("NotificationUser")

  @@map("users")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// REFRESH TOKENS  (auth module)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// [CHANGE 2] KEPT as a separate table — DID NOT collapse into users.refresh_token.
//
// Why the table wins over a single column on users:
//   1. Multi-device sessions. One user → many live tokens (laptop, phone,
//      browser). A single column would force one device at a time.
//   2. Per-device revocation. "Log out of this device only" is trivial with
//      a row-level delete; impossible with a single column.
//   3. Token rotation audit. Each refresh emits a new row and revokes the
//      previous one — a column can't preserve history.
//   4. Global sign-out. "Log out everywhere after password reset" = bulk
//      UPDATE … SET is_revoked = TRUE WHERE user_id = ? — one SQL statement.
//   5. Operational cost is minimal: ~N rows per active user, indexed by
//      token_hash and user_id, with periodic cleanup of expired/revoked rows.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model RefreshToken {
  id         String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  user_id    String   @db.Uuid
  /// SHA-256 of the refresh token — NEVER store the raw token.
  token_hash String   @unique
  expires_at DateTime
  created_at DateTime @default(now())
  /// Soft-revoke flag. A nightly job hard-deletes rows where
  /// is_revoked = TRUE OR expires_at < now() - interval '30 days'.
  is_revoked Boolean  @default(false)

  user User @relation(fields: [user_id], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@index([user_id, is_revoked])
  @@map("refresh_tokens")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.3  PROJECTS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Project {
  id                     String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id           String   @db.Uuid
  name                   String
  /// client | internal_bd | internal_build
  type                   String?
  /// active | paused | completed | archived
  status                 String?
  /// Layer 1 identity context injected into every AI thread
  brief                  String?
  system_instructions    String?
  default_model          String?
  owner_id               String   @db.Uuid
  clickup_link           String?
  slack_channel_link     String?
  // [CHANGE 3] fathom_link: String? → String[].
  // Fathom share URLs are regenerated on every re-share / re-record,
  // so a project accumulates multiple valid links over its lifetime.
  // Stored as a PostgreSQL text[]. Defaults to empty array.
  fathom_links           String[]
  vault_drive_link       String?
  /// OpenAI Vector Store ID — one per project, populated only for workspaces
  /// that ingest via the OpenAI path. Used by the File Search tool to scope
  /// semantic retrieval to this project. NULL for Anthropic-only workspaces
  /// (those use pgvector directly, scoped by project_id).
  openai_vector_store_id String?
  created_at             DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at             DateTime @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  owner     User      @relation("ProjectOwner", fields: [owner_id], references: [id])

  // [CHANGE 4] 1-to-many → one project can have many ProjectMember rows;
  // each row binds one User (from the same workspace, enforced via
  // ProjectMember.workspace_id) to this project with an access_level.
  project_members           ProjectMember[]
  project_custom_properties ProjectCustomProperty[]
  thread_groups             ThreadGroup[]
  threads                   Thread[]
  messages                  Message[]
  project_documents         ProjectDocument[]
  document_chunks           DocumentChunk[]
  attachments               Attachment[]
  vault_items               VaultItem[]
  skills                    Skill[]
  mcp_servers               McpServer[]
  document_templates        DocumentTemplate[]
  artifacts                 Artifact[]
  artifact_files            ArtifactFile[]
  scraping_events           ScrapingEvent[]
  usage_events              UsageEvent[]
  audit_log                 AuditLog[]
  mentions                  Mention[]

  @@index([workspace_id, status])
  @@map("projects")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.4  PROJECT_MEMBERS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// [CHANGE 4] Relationship shape (for reference, no structural change):
//   User 1─────* ProjectMember *─────1 Project
// One user can be a member of many projects; one project has many members.
// workspace_id is denormalised from both sides and MUST equal the user's
// workspace_id AND the project's workspace_id (enforced at the service layer
// and/or via a CHECK constraint in a raw migration).
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ProjectMember {
  id           String      @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String      @db.Uuid
  user_id      String      @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String      @db.Uuid
  // [CHANGE 5] access_level: String → AccessLevel enum (read_only | edit).
  access_level AccessLevel
  assigned_by  String      @db.Uuid
  assigned_at  DateTime    @default(now())

  project          Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace        Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  user             User      @relation("MemberUser", fields: [user_id], references: [id])
  assigned_by_user User      @relation("AssignedByUser", fields: [assigned_by], references: [id])

  @@unique([project_id, user_id])
  @@map("project_members")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.5  PROJECT_CUSTOM_PROPERTIES
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ProjectCustomProperty {
  id            String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id    String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id  String   @db.Uuid
  name          String
  /// text | number | date | single_select | multi_select | checkbox | person
  property_type String
  /// [{value, label, color}] for select types
  options       Json?
  sort_order    Int?
  created_by    String   @db.Uuid
  created_at    DateTime @default(now())

  project   Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("CustomPropertyCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])

  thread_property_values ThreadPropertyValue[]

  @@map("project_custom_properties")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.6  THREAD_GROUPS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ThreadGroup {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid
  name         String
  created_by   String   @db.Uuid
  created_at   DateTime @default(now())

  project   Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("ThreadGroupCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])

  threads Thread[]

  @@map("thread_groups")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.7  THREADS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Thread {
  id                    String    @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id            String    @db.Uuid
  workspace_id          String    @db.Uuid
  group_id              String?   @db.Uuid
  title                 String
  /// Strategy | Dev | Automation | Copy | Ads | Research | BD | Ops | Admin | Design | Proposal | SOW
  purpose_tag           String?
  /// active | archived
  status                String?   @default("active")

  system_prompt         String?
  created_by            String    @db.Uuid
  last_model_used       String?
  last_active_at        DateTime?
  /// Aggregated cost — updated per message response
  total_cost            Decimal?  @db.Decimal(10, 6)
  /// Stored compacted conversation summary for context window management
  compaction_summary    String?
  compaction_message_id String?   @db.Uuid
  created_at            DateTime  @default(now())
  updated_at            DateTime  @updatedAt

  project      Project      @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace    Workspace    @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  thread_group ThreadGroup? @relation(fields: [group_id], references: [id])
  creator      User         @relation("ThreadCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])

  messages               Message[]
  thread_property_values ThreadPropertyValue[]
  thread_active_skills   ThreadActiveSkill[]
  attachments            Attachment[]
  artifacts              Artifact[]
  artifact_files         ArtifactFile[]
  scraping_events        ScrapingEvent[]
  usage_events           UsageEvent[]
  mentions               Mention[]

  /// idx_threads_project — paginated thread list sorted by last active
  @@index([project_id, last_active_at(sort: Desc)])
  @@map("threads")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.8  THREAD_PROPERTY_VALUES
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ThreadPropertyValue {
  id          String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  thread_id   String @db.Uuid
  property_id String @db.Uuid
  /// The value supplied for this custom property on this thread. Shape depends
  /// on the parent property_type:
  ///   text              → "some string"
  ///   number            → 42
  ///   date              → "2025-10-14T00:00:00Z" (ISO)
  ///   single_select     → "option_value"
  ///   multi_select      → ["opt_a", "opt_b"]
  ///   checkbox          → true / false
  ///   person            → ["<user_uuid>", "<user_uuid>"]
  value       Json?

  thread   Thread                @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  property ProjectCustomProperty @relation(fields: [property_id], references: [id])

  @@unique([thread_id, property_id])
  @@map("thread_property_values")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2.9  MESSAGES
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Message {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  thread_id    String   @db.Uuid
  project_id   String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid
  /// user | assistant | system
  role         String
  content      String

  /// ⚠ Cannot be set by Prisma — create via raw SQL migration:
  ///   ALTER TABLE messages ADD COLUMN content_search_vector tsvector
  ///   GENERATED ALWAYS AS (to_tsvector('english', content)) STORED;

  /// anthropic | openai | google
  provider   String?
  model_name String?

  created_by    String   @db.Uuid
  token_in      Int?
  token_out     Int?
  /// Convenience cache: (token_in × price_in) + (token_out × price_out).
  /// Source of truth for finance is usage_events table — this column may be
  /// dropped in a future optimisation pass.
  cost_estimate Decimal? @db.Decimal(10, 6)
  /// TRUE if this row is a compaction summary record
  is_compacted  Boolean  @default(false)
  created_at    DateTime @default(now())

  thread    Thread    @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  project   Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("MessageCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])

  attachments          Attachment[]
  thread_active_skills ThreadActiveSkill[]
  artifacts            Artifact[]
  artifact_files       ArtifactFile[]
  usage_events         UsageEvent[]
  mentions             Mention[]

  /// idx_messages_thread — paginated message history
  @@index([thread_id, created_at])
  /// idx_messages_project — project-level message queries
  @@index([project_id, created_at])
  @@map("messages")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 3.1  PROJECT_DOCUMENTS  (unified source record for all document types)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ProjectDocument {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid

  /// upload | google_doc | vault | chat_upload | fathom_transcript |
  /// slack_thread | clickup_sync | firecrawl_web
  source_type String?
  title       String

  /// pdf | docx | txt | md | csv | xlsx | image | google_doc | html
  file_type       String?
  /// Enforced max 20 MB at API level
  file_size_bytes Int?

  /// s3 | google_drive | anthropic_files | external_url
  storage_type String?
  storage_key  String?

  /// Set when source_type = google_doc
  google_doc_id       String?
  original_url        String?
  external_source_url String?

  // ─── [CHANGE 6] Provider-specific file identifiers ─────────────────────────
  // All three are justified by the BYOK + dual-provider architecture
  // (see CIOS_Scraping_Implementation_Plan.docx §3 and §4). Per row, typically
  // only the columns for the active provider path are populated; they can
  // coexist only if the same document has been ingested into both pipelines.

  /// OpenAI Files API file_id, returned by POST /v1/files.
  /// Needed to (a) attach the file to the project's Vector Store via
  /// POST /v1/vector_stores/{id}/files, and (b) pass it as an input to
  /// Code Interpreter for deterministic file manipulation.
  /// Populated only on the OpenAI ingestion path; NULL otherwise.
  openai_file_id       String?

  /// Anthropic Files API file_id, returned by POST /v1/files (with the
  /// `anthropic-beta: files-api-2025-04-14` header).
  /// Enables the "create once, reference many" pattern: the same client
  /// brief can be referenced across dozens of threads by id alone, instead
  /// of re-encoding it as base64 in every request. For PDFs, this also
  /// unlocks Claude's native page-to-image vision pipeline.
  /// Populated only on the Anthropic ingestion path; NULL otherwise.
  anthropic_file_id    String?

  /// OpenAI Vector Store attachment ID, returned by
  /// POST /v1/vector_stores/{vector_store_id}/files.
  /// DISTINCT from openai_file_id — this id tracks the file's membership
  /// and indexing status *within the vector store*. Used to (a) poll
  /// GET /v1/vector_stores/{id}/files/{vs_file_id} until status = completed,
  /// and (b) detach the file from the store without deleting the underlying
  /// Files API object. Populated only on the OpenAI path.
  vector_store_file_id String?

  /// pending | processing | completed | failed.
  /// Ingestion status is driven by the n8n pipeline (not the NestJS app);
  /// the backend writes the initial `pending` state and n8n updates it.
  ingestion_status String?   @default("pending")
  /// Pinned docs always loaded in full at Layer 2 context assembly
  is_pinned        Boolean   @default(false)

  /// Flexible: page_count, word_count, last_modified, google_revision_id …
  metadata       Json?
  chunk_count    Int?
  last_synced_at DateTime?
  uploaded_by    String    @db.Uuid
  created_at     DateTime  @default(now())

  project   Project         @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace       @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  uploader  User            @relation("DocumentUploadedBy", fields: [uploaded_by], references: [id])

  document_chunks DocumentChunk[]
  attachments     Attachment[]
  vault_items     VaultItem[]

  @@map("project_documents")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 3.2  DOCUMENT_CHUNKS  (pgvector RAG — rows are NEVER hard-deleted)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model DocumentChunk {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid
  document_id  String   @db.Uuid
  /// Denormalised from parent document for query efficiency
  source_type  String?
  /// Sequential position within parent document (0-indexed)
  chunk_index  Int
  /// ~600 tokens with 100-token overlap
  content      String
  /// SHA-256 hash of normalised content — used for cross-source deduplication
  content_hash String

  /// TRUE when document is re-ingested. NEVER hard-delete these rows
  /// (foreign-key audit trail + embedding cost already paid).
  superseded Boolean  @default(false)
  created_at DateTime @default(now())

  project   Project         @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace       @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  document  ProjectDocument @relation(fields: [document_id], references: [id])

  /// idx_doc_chunks_project — scoped RAG retrieval
  @@index([project_id, superseded])
  @@map("document_chunks")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 3.3  ATTACHMENTS  (files attached to specific chat messages)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Attachment {
  id              String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  message_id      String   @db.Uuid
  thread_id       String   @db.Uuid
  project_id      String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id    String   @db.Uuid
  file_name       String?
  /// MIME type
  file_type       String?
  file_size_bytes Int?
  /// S3 object key
  storage_key     String?
  /// Links to ingestion record — nullable
  document_id     String?  @db.Uuid
  uploaded_by     String   @db.Uuid
  created_at      DateTime @default(now())

  message   Message          @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  thread    Thread           @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  project   Project          @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace        @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  document  ProjectDocument? @relation(fields: [document_id], references: [id])
  uploader  User             @relation("AttachmentUploadedBy", fields: [uploaded_by], references: [id])

  @@map("attachments")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 3.4  VAULT_ITEMS  (Client Vault structured document registry)

model VaultItem {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid

  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid
  /// Nullable — external-link-only items have no document record
  document_id  String?  @db.Uuid

  /// canonical | working_artifact

  /// sow | proposal | roadmap | strategy | brief | copy_draft |
  /// report | transcript | deliverable
  document_type String?

  /// s3 | google_drive | external
  storage_type  String?
  /// S3 object key or Google Drive file ID
  storage_key   String?
  external_link String?
  uploaded_by   String   @db.Uuid
  created_at    DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at    DateTime @updatedAt

  project   Project          @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace        @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  document  ProjectDocument? @relation(fields: [document_id], references: [id])
  uploader  User             @relation("VaultItemUploadedBy", fields: [uploaded_by], references: [id])

  @@map("vault_items")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 4.1  SKILLS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Skill {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL = workspace-scoped; non-null = project-scoped
  project_id   String? @db.Uuid

  /// Unique within workspace — kebab-case. Used for /skill lookup.
  name        String  @db.VarChar(64)
  /// Semantic routing description loaded during Phase 2 Discovery (~100 tokens)
  description String? @db.VarChar(1024)

  /// workspace | project (redundant with project_id nullable — explicit for query clarity)
  scope    String
  /// Automation | AI Dev | Brand | GTM | Full-Stack | Proposal | Onboarding | SOW | Custom
  category String?

  /// Full SKILL.md body — only loaded in Phase 4 Progressive Disclosure, never during Discovery
  content_md String?

  /// live | pending_approval | archived
  status String @default("pending_approval")

  /// If TRUE, auto-loaded at thread creation without explicit invocation
  auto_inject Boolean @default(false)

  /// Current live version number — incremented on every approved edit
  version Int @default(1)

  /// html | docx | pptx — enables document artifact generation pipeline
  output_type   String?
  /// References artifact_templates.slug
  template_slug String?
  schema_slug   String?

  created_by  String   @db.Uuid
  approved_by String?  @db.Uuid
  created_at  DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at  DateTime @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  project   Project?  @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("SkillCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])
  approver  User?     @relation("SkillApprovedBy", fields: [approved_by], references: [id])

  skill_versions       SkillVersion[]
  thread_active_skills ThreadActiveSkill[]
  artifacts            Artifact[]

  /// idx_skills_workspace — discovery query: all live skills for workspace
  @@index([workspace_id, status, scope])
  @@map("skills")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 4.2  SKILL_VERSIONS  (immutable snapshot before every live skill edit)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model SkillVersion {
  id             String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  skill_id       String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id   String   @db.Uuid
  version_number Int
  /// Complete SKILL.md body at this version — immutable once written
  content_md     String
  /// Optional description of what changed
  change_summary String?
  changed_by     String   @db.Uuid
  created_at     DateTime @default(now())

  skill           Skill     @relation(fields: [skill_id], references: [id])
  workspace       Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  changed_by_user User      @relation("SkillVersionChangedBy", fields: [changed_by], references: [id])

  @@map("skill_versions")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 4.3  THREAD_ACTIVE_SKILLS  (per-message skill injection tracking)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ThreadActiveSkill {
  id           String   @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  thread_id    String   @db.Uuid
  /// NULL = thread-session level; non-null = specific message
  message_id   String?  @db.Uuid
  skill_id     String   @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String   @db.Uuid

  /// auto_inject | manual | dependency
  invocation_type String

  /// User dismissed this skill for the current session (does not remove from library)
  dismissed   Boolean  @default(false)
  injected_at DateTime

  thread    Thread    @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  message   Message?  @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  skill     Skill     @relation(fields: [skill_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])

  @@map("thread_active_skills")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 5.1  MCP_SERVERS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model McpServer {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL = workspace-scoped; non-null = project-specific
  project_id   String? @db.Uuid

  name        String
  /// SSE endpoint URL
  url         String
  description String?

  /// oauth2 | api_key | none
  auth_method String?
  /// AES-256 encrypted — NEVER returned in API responses
  auth_config Json?

  /// [{name, description, inputSchema}]
  supported_tools Json?

  /// workspace | project
  scope String?

  /// active | inactive | pending_approval
  status String? @default("pending_approval")

  added_by    String   @db.Uuid
  approved_by String?  @db.Uuid
  created_at  DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at  DateTime @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  project   Project?  @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  adder     User      @relation("McpAddedBy", fields: [added_by], references: [id])
  approver  User?     @relation("McpApprovedBy", fields: [approved_by], references: [id])

  @@map("mcp_servers")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 6.1  ARTIFACT_TEMPLATES  (visual slot-filling template files)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ArtifactTemplate {
  id           String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String @db.Uuid

  name      String
  brand_tag String?

  /// html | docx | pptx
  output_type       String
  template_file_url String?
  thumbnail_url     String?

  /// [{name, type, description, maxLength, required}] injected into AI prompt
  schema_json Json

  /// Machine-readable identifier (e.g. ladder-proposal) — referenced by skills
  slug    String   @unique
  version Int      @default(1)

  /// active | pending_approval | archived
  status String? @default("pending_approval")

  created_by  String   @db.Uuid
  approved_by String?  @db.Uuid
  created_at  DateTime @default(now())
  updated_at  DateTime @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("ArtifactTemplateCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])
  approver  User?     @relation("ArtifactTemplateApprovedBy", fields: [approved_by], references: [id])

  artifacts Artifact[]

  @@map("artifact_templates")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 6.2  DOCUMENT_TEMPLATES  (Code Interpreter / python-docx generation specs)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model DocumentTemplate {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL = workspace-level (available to all projects)
  project_id   String? @db.Uuid

  template_name String

  /// proposal | sow | prd | report | brand_guidelines | case_study | custom
  document_type String

  /// Section ordering, heading hierarchy, required boilerplate, typography rules
  template_spec Json

  /// Base Python code fragment (python-docx branded styles) — injected into Code Interpreter prompt
  python_docx_snippet String?
  /// Optional reference to SKILL.md file for this document type
  skill_file_path     String?

  /// draft | active
  status String @default("draft")

  created_by  String   @db.Uuid
  approved_by String?  @db.Uuid
  created_at  DateTime @default(now())

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  project   Project?  @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  creator   User      @relation("DocumentTemplateCreatedBy", fields: [created_by], references: [id])
  approver  User?     @relation("DocumentTemplateApprovedBy", fields: [approved_by], references: [id])

  @@map("document_templates")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 6.3  ARTIFACTS  (generated artifact records with export URLs)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Artifact {
  id           String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  message_id   String @db.Uuid
  thread_id    String @db.Uuid
  project_id   String @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String @db.Uuid

  template_id String? @db.Uuid
  skill_id    String? @db.Uuid

  /// AI-returned structured JSON matching the template schema
  content_json  Json?
  /// Stored rendered HTML (HTML template type) — avoids re-rendering
  rendered_html String?
  /// S3 signed-URL base paths for each export format
  docx_url      String?
  pptx_url      String?
  /// PDF always generated as secondary format
  pdf_url       String?

  created_at DateTime @default(now())

  message   Message           @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  thread    Thread            @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  project   Project           @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace         @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  template  ArtifactTemplate? @relation(fields: [template_id], references: [id])
  skill     Skill?            @relation(fields: [skill_id], references: [id])

  @@map("artifacts")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 6.4  ARTIFACT_FILES  (persistent S3 binary file records)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ArtifactFile {
  id           String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String @db.Uuid
  thread_id    String @db.Uuid
  message_id   String @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String @db.Uuid

  /// e.g. Acme-Proposal-v1.docx
  file_name String
  /// docx | pptx | pdf | xlsx | html
  file_type String
  /// S3 object key
  storage_path String
  /// Permanent pre-signed URL with extended expiry (bypasses 20-min Code Interpreter expiry)
  download_url String?

  generated_by_model           String?
  generation_prompt_tokens     Int?
  generation_completion_tokens Int?
  cost_usd                     Decimal? @db.Decimal(10, 6)
  created_at                   DateTime @default(now())

  project   Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  thread    Thread    @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  message   Message   @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])

  @@map("artifact_files")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 7.1  SCRAPING_EVENTS  (audit trail for all web fetch / scrape events)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ScrapingEvent {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  project_id   String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL for background ingestion not triggered in a thread
  thread_id    String? @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL for automated / scheduled ingestion
  user_id      String? @db.Uuid

  /// web_fetch | web_search | firecrawl_scrape | firecrawl_crawl |
  /// google_doc_sync | fathom_ingest
  event_type String
  url        String?

  tokens_fetched         Int?
  /// NULL for OpenAI path (no dynamic filtering)
  tokens_after_filtering Int?
  /// Percentage token reduction from Anthropic dynamic filtering
  filter_savings_pct     Decimal? @db.Decimal(5, 2)

  /// success | failed | partial
  status        String
  error_message String?
  timestamp     DateTime

  project   Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  thread    Thread?   @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  user      User?     @relation("ScrapingEventUser", fields: [user_id], references: [id])

  @@map("scraping_events")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.1  USAGE_EVENTS  (granular per-API-call cost tracking)
// Source of truth for F13 Finance dashboard.
// messages.cost_estimate is a convenience cache only.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model UsageEvent {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL for workspace-level operations (e.g. admin embedding)
  project_id   String? @db.Uuid
  thread_id    String? @db.Uuid
  message_id   String? @db.Uuid
  /// NULL for automated background jobs
  user_id      String? @db.Uuid

  /// chat | embedding | file_search | code_interpreter | web_fetch |
  /// web_search | code_execution | files_upload
  event_type String

  /// anthropic | openai | google
  provider String
  model    String

  tokens_in         Int?
  tokens_out        Int?
  /// Anthropic prompt cache read tokens (billed at reduced rate)
  cache_tokens_read Int?
  cost_usd          Decimal? @db.Decimal(10, 6)
  timestamp         DateTime

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  project   Project?  @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  thread    Thread?   @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  message   Message?  @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  user      User?     @relation("UsageEventUser", fields: [user_id], references: [id])

  /// idx_usage_events_project — finance dashboard aggregations
  @@index([project_id, timestamp(sort: Desc)])
  @@map("usage_events")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.2  MODEL_PRICING  (admin-updatable — NEVER hardcode prices in app code)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ModelPricing {
  id String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid

  /// anthropic | openai | google
  provider   String
  /// Exact model identifier e.g. claude-sonnet-4-6
  model_name String

  price_per_1k_token_in  Decimal @db.Decimal(10, 8)
  price_per_1k_token_out Decimal @db.Decimal(10, 8)
  effective_from         DateTime

  /// Only one TRUE row per provider + model combination
  is_current Boolean @default(false)

  @@unique([provider, model_name, effective_from])
  @@map("model_pricing")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.3  AUDIT_LOG  (immutable — INSERT only, no UPDATE/DELETE, 12-month retention)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model AuditLog {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid
  /// NULL for system-automated events
  user_id      String? @db.Uuid
  project_id   String? @db.Uuid

  /// login | logout | thread_created | message_sent | file_upload | file_download |
  /// permission_change | project_created | project_archived | api_key_added |
  /// api_key_rotated | skill_created | skill_edited | skill_approved | mcp_added |
  /// mcp_approved | template_uploaded | mention_created | mention_acknowledged |
  /// search | mcp_tool_invoked | artifact_generated | document_scraped
  event_type String

  /// Structured context — query_hash (never plaintext query), model, cost, url …
  event_detail Json
  ip_address   String?

  /// Immutable — never updated
  created_at DateTime @default(now())

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  user      User?     @relation("AuditLogUser", fields: [user_id], references: [id])
  project   Project?  @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])

  /// idx_audit_log_workspace
  @@index([workspace_id, created_at(sort: Desc)])
  @@map("audit_log")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.4  API_KEYS  (BYOK — encrypted at rest, never returned after initial save)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model ApiKey {
  id           String @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String @db.Uuid

  /// anthropic | openai | google
  provider String

  /// AES-256 encrypted — NEVER logged or returned in API responses
  encrypted_key String

  /// connected | invalid | missing
  key_status        String
  added_by          String    @db.Uuid
  last_validated_at DateTime?
  created_at        DateTime  @default(now())
  updated_at        DateTime  @updatedAt

  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  adder     User      @relation("ApiKeyAddedBy", fields: [added_by], references: [id])

  @@unique([workspace_id, provider])
  @@map("api_keys")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.5  MENTIONS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Mention {
  id                   String    @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  message_id           String    @db.Uuid
  thread_id            String    @db.Uuid
  project_id           String    @db.Uuid
  workspace_id         String    @db.Uuid
  mentioned_user_id    String    @db.Uuid
  mentioned_by_user_id String    @db.Uuid
  acknowledged         Boolean   @default(false)
  acknowledged_at      DateTime?
  created_at           DateTime  @default(now())

  message           Message   @relation(fields: [message_id], references: [id])
  thread            Thread    @relation(fields: [thread_id], references: [id])
  project           Project   @relation(fields: [project_id], references: [id])
  workspace         Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])
  mentioned_user    User      @relation("MentionedUser", fields: [mentioned_user_id], references: [id])
  mentioned_by_user User      @relation("MentionedByUser", fields: [mentioned_by_user_id], references: [id])

  @@map("mentions")
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 8.6  NOTIFICATIONS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

model Notification {
  id           String  @id @default(dbgenerated("gen_random_uuid()")) @db.Uuid
  user_id      String  @db.Uuid
  workspace_id String  @db.Uuid

  /// mention | approval_request | system | skill_approved | mcp_approved | template_approved
  type           String
  /// UUID of the entity this notification points to (e.g. a Mention row, a
  /// Skill pending approval). Nullable because some notifications (e.g. generic
  /// "system" notices) don't map to a specific entity.
  reference_id   String? @db.Uuid
  /// Discriminator for reference_id — tells the client which table to look up
  /// when the user clicks the notification. Values: mention | skill | mcp |
  /// template | artifact. Paired with reference_id so the client can route
  /// deep-links without a second round-trip.
  reference_type String?

  title String
  body  String?
  read  Boolean  @default(false)

  created_at DateTime @default(now())

  user      User      @relation("NotificationUser", fields: [user_id], references: [id])
  workspace Workspace @relation(fields: [workspace_id], references: [id])

  @@index([user_id, read, created_at(sort: Desc)])
  @@map("notifications")
}

// ============================================================================
// RAW SQL — apply these in a manual migration AFTER prisma migrate dev
// (Prisma cannot generate DDL for pgvector, generated columns, or BM25 indexes)
// ============================================================================
//
// -- 1. Extensions (run once per database)
// CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS vector;       -- pgvector
// CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_search;    -- ParadeDB BM25
//
// -- 2. Generated tsvector column on messages
// ALTER TABLE messages
//   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS content_search_vector tsvector
//   GENERATED ALWAYS AS (to_tsvector('english', content)) STORED;
//
// -- 3. HNSW vector indexes (m=16, ef_construction=64)
// CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY cios_vec_messages
//   ON messages USING hnsw (embedding vector_cosine_ops)
//   WITH (m = 16, ef_construction = 64);
//
// CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY cios_vec_doc_chunks
//   ON document_chunks USING hnsw (embedding vector_cosine_ops)
//   WITH (m = 16, ef_construction = 64);
//
// CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY cios_vec_skills
//   ON skills USING hnsw (embedding vector_cosine_ops)
//   WITH (m = 16, ef_construction = 64);
//
// -- 4. ParadeDB BM25 indexes (one per workspace for IDF isolation — example for a workspace UUID)
// -- Replace <workspace_uuid> with actual workspace IDs, or create a global index first:
// CALL paradedb.create_bm25(
//   table_name => 'messages',
//   index_name => 'cios_search_messages',
//   key_field  => 'id',
//   text_fields => paradedb.field('content') || paradedb.field('role')
// );
// CALL paradedb.create_bm25(
//   table_name => 'threads',
//   index_name => 'cios_search_threads',
//   key_field  => 'id',
//   text_fields => paradedb.field('title', tokenizer => paradedb.tokenizer('default', fast => true))
// );
// CALL paradedb.create_bm25(
//   table_name => 'skills',
//   index_name => 'cios_search_skills',
//   key_field  => 'id',
//   text_fields => paradedb.field('name', boost => 5.0) || paradedb.field('content_md')
// );
// CALL paradedb.create_bm25(
//   table_name => 'mcp_servers',
//   index_name => 'cios_search_mcp_servers',
//   key_field  => 'id',
//   text_fields => paradedb.field('name') || paradedb.field('description')
// );
// CALL paradedb.create_bm25(
//   table_name => 'vault_items',
//   index_name => 'cios_search_vault_items',
//   key_field  => 'id',
//   text_fields => paradedb.field('title')
// );
//
// -- 5. PostgreSQL RLS — enable on every table (enforce workspace_id isolation)
// ALTER TABLE workspaces ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
// ALTER TABLE users ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
// -- ... repeat for all 28 tables + refresh_tokens
//
// -- 6. audit_log permissions — INSERT only for the API app role
// REVOKE UPDATE, DELETE ON audit_log FROM <api_app_role>;
// REVOKE UPDATE, DELETE ON document_chunks FROM <api_app_role>;
// ============================================================================
</file>

</files>
